Author: Evan Ward <evan.ward@nrl.navy.mil>

    Fix missing doc of default data context use
    
    The toString() methods of CartesianOrbit, FieldCartesianOrbit,
    TimeStampedFieldPVCoordinates, and TimeStampedPVCoordinates used the
    default data context by appending a date to a string. Modified
    CartesianOrbit to only use the six defining elements like is done for
    the other subclasses of Orbit. Added a toString(TimeScale) method to
    TimeStampedPVCoordinates and modified the field version to call it.
    
    Part of #607

commit 9ecd58cf41882814bcee18b8a91e38ad8a9951f4
Author: Evan Ward <evan.ward@nrl.navy.mil>
Date:   2019-12-12 11:07:07 -0500

    Fix adding EOP loaders before leap seconds
    
    In Orekit 10.0 it is possible to add default and custom EOP loaders
    before leap seconds are available to the application. Before this commit
    UTC was a constructor argument to the loaders so it was needed before
    the loaders were added. Restored the 10.0 behavior by changing the
    constructor argument to a UTC supplier that is only accessed when it is
    first needed.
    
    Part of #607

commit ac5fb92c8abda5dc3193288642f909931ce8863a
Author: Evan Ward <evan.ward@nrl.navy.mil>
Date:   2019-11-20 11:25:40 -0500

    Update AbsoluteDate for TimeScales
    
    Updated AbsoluteDate to provide alternatives to using the default
    DataContext, including the constant epochs. Also updated
    FieldAbsoluteDate and all classes that used the methods dependent on the
    default DataContext. Added AbsoluteDate.ARBITRARY_EPOCH to replace
    places J2000_EPOCH was used but the point in time was irrelevant. Added
    DateTimeComponents.JULIAN_EPOCH to use it separated from the default TT
    time scale.
    
    Updated the TLEConverterTest to use a looser tolerance. The changes
    resulted in a 1 ulp difference in one of the calculations in
    SDP4/DeepSDP4. The test had been using a tolerance less than its
    convergence threshold which makes the pass/fail fairly arbitrary.
    
    Part of #607

commit 50671c7f5c91de069e30cc15dac959d8f6c8aa36
Author: Guilhem Bonnefille <guilhem.bonnefille@c-s.fr>
Date:   2019-10-09 18:59:47 +0200

    Replace sleep with timeout
    
    Using sleep imposes to wait the given amount of time
    even if the result is available sooner.
    Using the TimeOut, the get is released as soon as
    the result is available. Thus, we can use a greater value
    for the timeout to handle the case the execution
    is exceptionnaly long, without any impact on faster conditions.

Author: Sébastien Dinot <sebastien.dinot@c-s.fr>
Date:   2019-08-26 12:59:54 +0200

    Install in local Maven repo the binary archive produced by develop branch
    
    Projects which depend on Orekit, such as Rugged, need the latest snapshot
    archive to be installed in the local Maven cache. To avoid confusion
    and non-reproducible results that could come out from archives generated
    by different branches, only the develop branch installs its archive.

commit 78fcc0c5482d0d367ca3acc4b394f4ae4128daf3
Author: Luc Maisonobe <luc@orekit.org>
Date:   2019-06-14 20:30:33 +0200

    Added an aiming direction that diverts singularity outside of a zone.
    
    This is mainly useful when sampling areas of interest that cover the
    pole as the pole is singular for classical aiming directions (constant
    azimuth or along track).
    
    Thanks to Pascal for the very clever idea of diverting singularity!
    
    Fixes #547

commit 3403f14e61e46abd5810b066b99d5b7c6fec122a
Author: Luc Maisonobe <luc@orekit.org>
Date:   2019-06-14 14:58:32 +0200

    Added safety check for impossible sampling of singular points.
    
    As per Brouwer's hairy ball theorem, any vector field on the 2-sphere
    has at least one zero. This implies that any implementation of
    TileAiming interface has at least one points where the aiming direction
    cannot be computed. The most typical example is aiming always towards
    North pole, for which both poles are singular points.

commit ed7556853b87c4b12a7f94717e56255a4f2b840f
Author: Luc Maisonobe <luc@orekit.org>
Date:   2019-05-15 15:09:25 +0200

    Added on the fly shrinking of search ellipsoid on LAMBDA method.
    
    This *vastly* improves search time. As an example, the test for random
    problems was pushed up to dimension 20 (previously the test was limited
    to dimension 10 so it completes in reasonable time). Without ellipsoid
    shrinking, it involved hundreds of millions of candidate points for some
    problems and I interrupted it after 45 minutes. Now it involves at most
    20 candidate points for all problems and the test completes in 3.6
    seconds...

commit c1c411faf8bb6e79e3a0ee7e24042da8c5e9299f
Author: Evan Ward <evan.ward@nrl.navy.mil>
Date:   2019-05-14 09:07:38 -0400

    Change itrf-versions.conf to match based on prefix
    
    Previous method of matching based on a regular expression could lead to an
    application hang if an crafted file was loaded. Since these files can be loaded
    from the network the matching mechanism was changed to avoid a potential denial
    of service. Also updated the separator in ZipJarCrawler to match the convention
    in JarURLConnection. Added some test cases.
    
    Fixes #543

Author: Evan Ward <evan.ward@nrl.navy.mil>
Date:   2019-05-10 17:09:49 +0200

    Merge branch 'mailmap-update' into 'develop'
    
    Updated list of canonical names and email addresses of contributors
    
    The file `.mailmap`, which enables displaying the canonical name and email addresse of the contributors in the Git log, was outdated. Before its update, 49 different authors appeared in the log, after the update, only 33 authors appear.
    
    For your information, Git can be configured to to use the `.mailmap` file by default in log through to the command below:
    
    ```bash
    git config --global log.mailmap true
    ```
    
    See merge request orekit/orekit!4
